Function: bool func0(const char *brackets) {
  int level = 0;
  for (int i = 0; i < strlen(brackets); i++) {
    if (brackets[i] == '(')
      level += 1;
    if (brackets[i] == ')')
      level -= 1;

}

    found = 0;

        found = 1;
        break;
      }

    }

}

Function: int func0(const char *date) {
  int mm, dd, yy;
  if (strlen(date) != 10)
    return 0;
  for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
    if (i == 2 || i == 5) {
      if (date[i] != '-')
        return 0;
    } else {
      if (date[i] < '0' || date[i] > '9')
        return 0;
    }
  }
  char str_month[3] = {date[0], date[1], '\x00'};
  char str_day[3] = {date[3], date[4], '\x00'};
  char str_year[5] = {date[6], date[7], date[8], date[9], '\x00'};
  mm = atoi(str_month);
  dd = atoi(str_day);
  yy = atoi(str_year);
  if (mm < 1 || mm > 12)
    return 0;
  if (dd < 1 || dd > 31)
    return 0;
  if ((mm == 4 || mm == 6 || mm == 9 || mm == 11) && dd == 31)
    return 0;
  if (mm == 2 && dd > 29)
    return 0;
  return 1;
}

Function: int func0(int lst[], int size) {
  int largest = 0, sum = 0, num, temp;
  for (int i = 0; i < size; ++i) {
    num = lst[i];
    if (num > 1) {
      int prime = 1;
      for (int j = 2; j * j <= num; ++j) {
        if (num % j == 0) {
          prime = 0;
          break;
        }
      }
      if (prime) {
        largest = num > largest ? num : largest;
      }
    }
  }
  while (largest > 0) {
    sum += largest % 10;
    largest /= 10;
  }
  return sum;
}

    return "No";

  if (strcmp(last, ".txt") != 0 && strcmp(last, ".exe") != 0 &&
      strcmp(last, ".dll") != 0)
    return "No";
  for (int i = 0; i < length; i++) {

      num_digit++;
    if (file_name[i] == '.')
      num_dot++;
  }
  if (num_digit > 3 || num_dot != 1)
    return "No";
  return "Yes";
}

        is_palindrome = 0;

Function: int *func0(int n) {

  }
  return out;

Function: char *func0(int n, int m) {
  if (n > m)
    return "-1";
  int num = (m + n) / 2;
  char *out = (char *)malloc(33);
  out[0] = '\x00';
  int index = 32;
  out[index--] = '\x00';
  do {
    out[index--] = '0' + num % 2;
    num /= 2;
  } while (num > 0);
  return &out[index + 1];
}

  }

  }
  return out;

Function: int func0(int *arr, int arr_size) {
  if (arr_size == 0)
    return -32768;
  int sum = 0, prods = 1, i;
  for (i = 0; i < arr_size; i++) {
    sum += abs(arr[i]);
    if (arr[i] == 0)
      prods = 0;
    if (arr[i] < 0)
      prods = -prods;
  }
  return sum * prods;
}
